          <!-- note resp="Harshal Bhatt" Regarding 6.39: <p>Missing verses 109ab, 110cd, 114cd,
              115ab, 116cd, 117, 118, 119ab , 121cd, 122, 123ab, 125cd, 130, 131, 132, 133,
              134ab, 135cd, 136, 137ab, 144ab, 147cd, 148ab, 137cd, 167, 171cd, 172, 173, 174,
              190, 191, 193cd, 195, 196, 197, 198ab, 200cd, 201ab, 202ab, 204cd, 205, 206,
              207, 211cd, 216ab, 219, 220, 221, 222, 223, 224, 225, 226, 227, 228, 229ab,
              218cd, 232cd, 233, 234, 235, 236, 237, 238, 239, 240, 241, 242, 243, 244, 253cd,
              254cd, 255, 256, 257, , 258, 264, 266ab, 267cd, 268ab, 277, 278, 279, 280ab,
              281ab, 284cd, 286ab, 295-318, 319cd, 323</p>
            <p>Additions 124a, 135a, 158a, 160, 201a-201c, 210a-210e, 232a-232b, 254a-254c,
              273a-273g, 294a-294j, 320a-320b</p>
            <p>- Chapter begins from verse no 104, folio no. 180r</p>
            <p>- Verse 134ab is given after 128</p>
            <p>- There are two folios named 183v. In the first 183v folio, there are 7 verses.
              Content of these 7 verses (273a to 273g) seems different.</p>
            <p>- Content of 294a to 294j, match with Cakradatta of Cakrapaṇḍita</p>
       -->

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.1">athāto jvarapratiṣedhaṃ nāmādhyāyaṃ vyākhyāsyāmaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.2">atha khalu va<cb n="1"/>tsasuśruta </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.3">yenāmṛtam apām madhyād uddhṛtaṃ pūrvajanmani ||
            <caesura/>
             yato maratvaṃ samprāptās tridaśās tridiveśvarāḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.4">siṣyās tan deva<cb n="2"/>m āsīnaṃ prapacchas suśrutādayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vraṇasyopadravāḥ proktā vraṇinām apy ataḥ paraṃ</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.5">sāmā<lb n="6"/>sato vyāsataś ca vrūhi no bhiṣajām varaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             upadraveṇa juṣṭasya vraṇaḥ kṛcchreṇa sidhyati ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.6"><lb n="1"/>upadravas tu vraṇinaḥ kṛcchrasādhyatamo mataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             prakṣīṇavalamāṃsasya śeṣadhātuparikṣayāt ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.7ab">tasmād upadravāṃ kṛ<cb n="2"/>tsnān vadasva vadatāṃ varaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.8">jvaram ādau pravakṣyāmi sa rogānīkarāṭ smṛtaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.9">rudra<milestone facs="168r IMG_0105.JPG" n="168r"
              unit="digital-image"/><pb facs="173" n="168r"/><lb n="1"
              />kopā<unclear>gnisaṃbhūta</unclear>s sarvabhūtapratāpanaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tais tai nāmabhir anyeṣāṃ satvānāṃ parikīrtya<cb n="1"/>te ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.10">janmādau nidhane caiva bhavatīha na saṃśayaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             ataḥ sarvavikārāṇāṃ jvaro rājā prakīrttitaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.11">ṛte de<cb n="2"/>vamanuṣyebhyo nānyo viṣahate tu taṃ </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.13">svedoparodhas santāpaḥ sarvaṅgagrahaṇan tathā ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.14"><lb n="2"/>yugapad yatra roge tu jvara ity upadiśyate |
            <caesura/>
             doṣaiḥ pṛthak samastaiś ca dvaṃdvar āgantur e<cb n="1"/>va ca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.15">anekakāraṇotpannas smṛtas tv aṣṭavidhau jvaraḥ |
            <caesura/>
             doṣāḥ prakupitā gāḍham apathyāhārasevinaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.16">vyā<unclear>pya</unclear>deha<cb n="2"/>m aśeṣeṇa jvaram āpādayanti
            ha |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.19cd">a<choice>
              <corr>dhi</corr>
              <orig>pi</orig>
            </choice>mithyā<pc> </pc>prayuktaiś ca snehādyaiḥ karmabhir nṛṇāṃ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.20">vivi<lb n="3"/>dhād abhighātāc ca rogotthānāt prapākataḥ |
            <caesura/>
             śramāt kṣayād ajīrṇṇāc ca viṣāt sāmarttu<cb n="1"/>prayayāt |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.21">oṣadhīpuṣpagandhāc ca kāyān nakṣatrapīḍayā |.
            <caesura/>
             abhiṣāpābhicārābhyāṃ manobhūtābhiśaṅkayā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.22">strīṇā<cb n="2"/>m avaprajātānāṃ prajātānān tathāhitaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             stanyāvataraṇai caiva jvarau doṣaiḥ prakupyati ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.23"><lb n="4"/>tair vegavadbhir vahudhā
              samu<del>bhrā</del><unclear>dbha</unclear>ntair vimārgagaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             vikṣipyamāṇontaragnir bhava<cb n="1"/>ty āśur vahiścaraḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.24">ruṇaddhi cāpy apāṃ dhātuṃ yasmāt tasmāj jvarāturaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             bhava<add place="below-margin">tya</add>ty uṣṇagātraś ca svidyate na ca sarvaśaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.25"><cb n="2"/>śramoratrivivarṇṇatvavairasyaṃ nayanaplavaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             icchādveṣau vahuś cāpi śītavātātapā<lb n="5"/>diṣu |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.26">jṛṃbhoṅgamardo gurutā romaharṣo 'rucis tamaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             apraharṣaś ca śītaś ca bha<cb n="1"/>vaty utpatsyati jvare |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.27">sāmānyato viśeṣas tu jṛṃbhoty arthaṃ samīraṇāt |
            <caesura/>
             pittān nayanayo dāhaḥ | kaphād aṃnā<cb n="2"/>rucis tathā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.28">sarvaliṅgasamāvāyas sarvadoṣaprakopaje |
            <caesura/>
             rupair anyarābhyān tu saṃ<lb n="6"/>sṛṣṭadvaṃdvajaṃ viduḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.29">vepathur viṣamo vegaḥ kaṇṭhoṣṭhapariśoṣaṇaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             nidrānā<cb n="1"/>śaḥ kṣayastaṃbho gātrāṇāṃ raukṣyam eva ca ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.30">śiroruggātrarugvakravairasyaṃ gāḍhaviṭkatā |
            <caesura/>
             śūlādhmānajṛṃ<cb n="2"/>bhaṇañ ca bhavaty anilaje jvare ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.31">vegatīkṣau mahādāhā nidrālpaś ca tathā vamī ||
            <caesura/>
            <milestone facs="168_v IMG_0107.JPG" n="168_v" unit="digital-image"/><pb facs="174"
              n="168_v"/><lb n="1"/>kaṇṭhoṣṭhamukhanāsānāṃ svedaḥ pākaś ca jāyate ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.32">pralāpo vaktrakaṭutā mūrcchā dāho ma<cb n="1"/>das tṛṣā |
            <caesura/>
             pītavinmūtranetratvaṃ paittike bhrama eva ca ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.32a">stemityaṃ stimito vega ālasyaṃ madhurāsyatā |
            <caesura/>
             śuklamū<cb n="2"/>trapurīṣatvaṃ staṃbhas tṛptir athāpi ca ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.33">gauravaṃ śītam u<unclear>tkle</unclear>do romaharṣotinidra<lb n="2"
            />tā ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.34">pratiśyāyo ruciḥ kāsaḥ kaphajekṣṇoś ca śuklatā ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.38">sarvajaḥ sarvaliṅgas tu viśe<cb n="2"/>ṣaṃ cātra me śṛṇu |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.39">nāty uṣṇaśītolpasaṃjño bhrāntapekṣī hatasvaraḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.40">śvasan nipatitiḥ śete pralāpopadravāyutaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.41"><cb n="2"/>tam abhinyāsam ity āhur hatojasam athāpare |
            <caesura/>
             sannipātajvaraḥ kṛcchram asādhyam apare<lb n="3"/> viduḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.45">saptame divase prāpte <del>rsa</del>daśame dvādaśe pi vā ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.46">punar ghorataro bhūtvā praśa<cb n="1"/>maṃ yānti hanti vā |
            <caesura/>
             dvidoṣocchrayaliṅgās tu dvaṃdvajas trividhaḥ smṛtaḥ ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.47">tṛṣṇā mūrcchā bhramo dāhaḥ svapnanāśaḥ śiro<cb n="2"/>rujaḥ |
            <caesura/>
             kaṇṭhasya śoṣo vamathur lomaharṣorucis tamaḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.48">parvabhedaś ca jṛṃbhā ca vāta<lb n="4"/>pittajvarākṛtiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             staimityaṃ sarvāṇāṃ bhedo nidrā gaurava eva ca |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.49">śirograhaḥ pra<cb n="1"/>tiśyāyaḥ śleṣmavātajvarākṛtiḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.50">liptatiktāsyatās taṃdrā mohaḥ kāso rucis tṛṣā ||
            <caesura/>
             muhur dāho muhuḥ śī<cb n="2"/>ta śleṣmapittajvarākṛtiḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.57">vātādhikātvāt pravadanti tajjñās tṛtīyakaś cāpi catu<lb n="5"
            />rthakaṃ vā |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.57.add"> santāpapānātyayasaṃbha<unclear>ñca</unclear> pittādhikatvāt
            pravadanti tajjñāḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.58">pralepaka<cb n="1"/>ñ cāpi valāsakañ ca kaphādhikatvena vadanti
            tajjñāḥ |
            <caesura/>
             mu<del><unclear>tva</unclear></del>ktvānuvandhaṃ viṣamajvarā ye prāyena te
              dvaṃdvasamutthitā<cb n="2"/>s tu ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.59">tvaksthau śleṣmānilau śītam ādau janayato jvare |
            <caesura/>
             tayoḥ praśāntayoḥ pi<lb n="6"/>ttamante dāhaṃ karoti ca ||</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.39.60">karoty ādau tathā pittaṃ tvaksthaṃ dāham iti sthitiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             tasmiṃ<cb n="1"/>praśānte tv itarau śītamante ca kurvataḥ |</l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.8"> nimbāmbuccharditavataḥ ka<lb n="7"/><unclear reason="faded">phaje

              cert="unknown" reason="faded">kṛtam evam upakrameta |</unclear>
          </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.9"> drākṣāpaṭolaviḍavetrakarīranimbamūrvābhayākṣabadarāgalakendravṛkṣāḥ
            |
            <caesura/>
             bījaiḥ karañjanṛpavṛkṣabhavaiś ca piṣṭai<cb n="2"/> lehaṃ pacet surabhimūtrayutaṃ
            yathāvat | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.10"> mustāvacākaṭukarohiṇi<g ref="#newa-placeholder-mark"/><milestone
              facs="200r IMG_0058.JPG" n="200r" unit="digital-image"/><pb facs="249" n="200r"/><lb
              n="1"/><unclear cert="unknown" reason="faded">nirdahanyas tulyātha vāpi
              rajanābhayasaṃprayuktā |</unclear>
            <caesura/>
            <unclear cert="unknown" reason="faded"> mūtre vike dviradamūtrayutāḥ paced vā pāṭhāsamām
              ativiṣāṃ <cb n="1"/>rajanāñ ca mukhyāṃ |</unclear>
          </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.11"> maṇḍūkim arkam amṛtāṃ raśalāṃgalākhyāṃ mūtre paceta mahiṣasya
            vidhāṇavidvān |
            <caesura/>
             etān na santi caturo bhyasatas tu lehān gulmāruciś ca śi<cb n="2"/>khisādahṛdāmayāś ca
            | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.12"> sātmyāsvadeśacaritāṃ vividhāṃś ca bhakṣyāṃ pānāni
            mūlaphalaṣāḍavarogayogāṃ |
            <caesura/>
             seved ra<lb n="2"/><unclear reason="faded">sāṃś ca vividhāṃ</unclear> vividhaiḥ
            prakārair bhuñjīta vāpi laghurūkṣamanaḥsukhāni | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.13"> āsthāpanaṃ vividham atra virecana<cb n="1"/>ñ ca kuryān mṛdūni
            śirasaś ca virecanāni |
            <caesura/>
             trīṇy ūṣaṇāni triphalāṃ rajanīdvayañ ca cūrṇṇīkṛtāni yavaśūkavimiśritāni | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.14"> kṣaudrāyutāni vitaren mukha<cb n="2"/>dhāvanārthaṃm anyāni
            tiktakaṭukāni ca bheṣajāni |
            <caesura/>
             mustādirājaphalavargadaśāṃgasiddhaḥ kvāthair jayen madhuyutai<lb n="3"/>r vividhaiś ca
            lehaiḥ || </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.15"> mūtrāsavair guḍakṛtaiś ca tathāpy ariṣṭaiḥ kṣārāsavaiś ca
            madhumādhavatulyagandhaiḥ |
            <caesura/>
             syād eṣa <cb n="1"/>eva kaphavātaharo vidhiś ca | śātiṃ gate hutabhuji praśamāya tasya
            | </l>

          <l xml:id="SS.6.57.16"> icchāvināśabhayajeṣu ca bādhakeṣu | bhāvād bhavāya vitaret khalu
              śalyatā<cb n="2"/>pān |
            <caesura/>
             artheṣu cātipatiteṣu punarbhavāya paurāṇikaśrutimukhair avamānayeta iti || kāyaci || 20
            || 0 || </l>

            <lb n="4"/>cchardi hikkā śvāsakāsaḥ svaraghātam athāparaṃ |
            <caesura/>
             pratiśyāyaḥ krimiś caiva sodāvarttā visūcikā |
